fornecer informações sobre a visibilidade do painel.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5acea-349">Additionally, an <a visibility.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5acea-350">O host deve implementar <a href="/previous-versions/windows/internet-explorer/ie-developer/platform-apis/cc678966(v=vs.85)"><strong>QueryService</strong></a> com <strong>SID_EXPLORERPANEVISIBILITY</strong> como a ID do serviço.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5acea-350">The host should implement <a ID.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5acea-351">O host deve estar na cadeia de sites.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5acea-351">The host must be in the site chain.</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="5acea-352">A implementação de <a href="/windows/desktop/api/shobjidl_core/nn-shobjidl_core-iexplorerpanevisibility"><strong>IExplorerPaneVisibility</strong></a> é recuperada
